CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS farmer (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), age INT, gender VARCHAR(10), phone_number VARCHAR(15))</t><stat>UPDATE farmer SET age=35, phone_number='123-456-7890' WHERE id=3;</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS machinery (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), type VARCHAR(50), condition VARCHAR(50))
